###############################################################################
# Weak Zones for Ridges and Fractures of Earth
###############################################################################

Given by Mike is a file `<CONTOURS>.xy` that contains contours of the fault
lines at the surface and information on propagation into the earth.

The point cloud is generated by the script
  $ perl generate_earth.pl <CONTOURS>.xy <DEPTHFILE>.dat <BETWEEN_DEPTH> <OUT_REFINE>

where 
  <DEPTHFILE>.dat --- contains depth values [km] at which points are generated
  <BETWEEN_DEPTH> --- number of depths in beetween points for numerical scheme
  <OUT_REFINE>    --- refinement in between data points

additionally, the `generate_earth.pl` skript has a parameter
  <REFINE_FACTOR> --- factor for points in <CONTOURS>.xy

###############################################################################

Command used for script:

  $ perl generate_earth.pl input_earth/Ridges_AND_Fractures.xy input_earth/depths1_2km.dat 5 14

Script output:
